				limit = {

						value = 7

				set_variable = { 
					which = ges
					which = gel

			else = { 
				if = { 
					limit = {

						}

				limit = { 
					NOT = {

							value = 6

				trigger_switch = {

					TN_Harbour_Major = {

					limit = {

						which = ges
						value = 4

				limit = {

			while = { 
				limit = { 
					check_variable = { 
						which = gek
						which = ger
					}
					NOT = { 
						check_variable = { 
							which = gch
							value = 7
						}
					}
				}
				change_variable = { 
					which = gch
					value = 1
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						check_variable = { 
							which = gch
							value = 7
						}
					}
					set_variable = { 
						which = ger
						which = gek
					}
				}
				else = { 
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { 
								which = gch
								value = 3
							}
						}
						if = { 
							limit = { 
								check_variable = { 
									which = gch
									value = 4
								}
							}
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									check_variable = { 
										which = gch
										value = 6
									}
								}
								set_variable = { 
									which = ger
									value = 60
								}
							}
